title: "trying to recover files from a failed hard drive using Ubuntu 13.1"
date: 2014-04-08

---

### Post by JustMyAlias on 2014-04-08
I have Ubuntu loaded on a bootable USB.
The failed hard drive is in a BlacX docking station, but I am still unable to access the files.
At first, it said the drive was unmounted, then it said it was mounted to rofs.
Can someone please help me?
I really know nothing about Ubuntu.
TIA!

---

### Post by Double.J on 2014-04-08
Hi there!

very sorry to hear about your situation.

try downloading testdisk from the software center. If it does not come up, click on sources and make sure 'universe' is enabled.

it runs from the terminal if i remember.

i have has lick in he past using the [photorec]("http://www.cgsecurity.org/wiki/TestDisk_Livecd") live cd directly.

best of luck!

Jj

---

### Post by XBNCPRk on 2014-04-08
Im not sure what the problem youre asking about is? rofs is read-only file system, and if it says its mounted, the files will be available wherever it says it has mounted it to. 

 If you are unsure where it has mounted to, you can use the Disk Utility (click the dash button on the top right, and type disk utility in the search box). Along the left-hand side it will list the various drives on the system, including any that arent mounted yet. Pick the one that is the drive in question, and on the right-hand pane it will tell you and give you a link to where it is mounted, or will give you the option to mount it.
